### Solving Part 2 ^aX4iv0IP

**Problem:** Berechne, nach wie viel Sekunden die Rakete auf dem Boden auftrifft. Erkläre, welche Stelle damit berechnet wird. ^NJAlRwIg

Given: ^3qlUaKil

- \( h(t) = v_0 \cdot t - \frac{g}{2} \cdot t^2 \) ^DWru2zgj

- \( g = 9.81 \, \frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{s}^2} \) ^ShLKB7fI

- \( v_0 = 80 \, \frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{s}} \) ^rscpoHjY

The height \( h(t) \) when the rocket hits the ground is 0 meters. ^Ir2SHsjr

Therefore, set \( h(t) = 0 \) and solve for \( t \): ^AflBxmRd

\[ 0 = v_0 \cdot t - \frac{g}{2} \cdot t^2 \] ^SeBnDHiE

Substitute the given values: ^l4v1qDfW

\[ 0 = 80t - \frac{9.81}{2} t^2 \] ^89qCb4wp

\[ 0 = 80t - 4.905 t^2 \] ^BInXhfUd

This is a quadratic equation of the form: ^cm63tVD0

\[ -4.905 t^2 + 80t = 0 \] ^gievAvdh

Factor out \( t \): ^D7SSAmO3

\[ t(-4.905t + 80) = 0 \] ^EFlPQ8vl

This gives two solutions: ^kicLDabs

\[ t = 0 \quad \text{(initial time, not relevant)} \] ^vJEn4DvM

\[ -4.905t + 80 = 0 \] ^qe6YNPeK

Solve for \( t \): ^rHi75MAV

\[ 4.905t = 80 \] ^7mbIW1RB

\[ t = \frac{80}{4.905} \] ^2yh834hJ

\[ t \approx 16.31 \, \text{seconds} \] ^dwycgLza

### Solving Part 5 ^BuXSTHtX

**Problem:** Mit welcher Anfangsgeschwindigkeit \( v_0 \) müsste die Rakete abgeschossen werden, damit sie um 1 Sekunde früher auf dem Boden auftrifft? ^MwHyvpOk

Given: ^mrePR2Wv

- The original time to hit the ground is 16.31 seconds. ^2w1LGOTr

- We want it to hit the ground 1 second earlier: \( 16.31 - 1 = 15.31 \) seconds. ^hEdWx2gL

The height function is: ^OljD07jR

\[ h(t) = v_0 \cdot t - \frac{9.81}{2} \cdot t^2 \] ^en44A6yU

Set \( h(t) = 0 \) and solve for the new \( v_0 \): ^Lyrnlg4l

\[ 0 = v_0 \cdot 15.31 - \frac{9.81}{2} \cdot (15.31)^2 \] ^XCMD9x78

Solve for \( v_0 \): ^xoX8udKz

\[ v_0 \cdot 15.31 = \frac{9.81}{2} \cdot (15.31)^2 \] ^rXuWg10H

\[ v_0 = \frac{\frac{9.81}{2} \cdot (15.31)^2}{15.31} \] ^14KQXxjN

Calculate the new \( v_0 \): ^diw8wG2P

\[ v_0 = \frac{4.905 \cdot (15.31)^2}{15.31} \] ^r6uVTd6f

\[ v_0 = 4.905 \cdot 15.31 \] ^MR0rM35p

\[ v_0 \approx 75.08 \, \frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{s}} \] ^9JIKgaSQ

Therefore, the rocket would need to be launched with an initial velocity of approximately \( 75.08 \, \frac{\mathrm{m}}{\mathrm{s}} \) for it to hit the ground 1 second earlier. ^mJz1cUsj
